## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) numerical expression is:
$$-0.33236 \cdot A^2 - 0.33236 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.07071 \cdot t} + 0.13650 \cdot \sin(\sqrt{A})$$

The key terms are:
1. **$A^2$ term**: $-0.33236 \cdot A^2$
2. **$A \cdot e^{-ct}$ term**: $-0.33236 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.07071t}$
3. **$\sin(\sqrt{A})$ term**: $0.13650 \cdot \sin(\sqrt{A})$

The critical component is the **$\sin(\sqrt{A})$** term. Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce this term.

Most candidates contain terms like `sqrt(A)*c0*exp(A*c1)`. Setting c1=0 gives `c0*sqrt(A)`, which is NOT $\sin(\sqrt{A})$. Setting c0=0 eliminates it entirely.

**Candidates with sin terms** (10, 14, 26, 30, 35):
- **10, 14**: Have `sin(A*c6 + c7)` — this is $\sin(c_6 A + c_7)$, not $\sin(\sqrt{A})$. Cannot match.
- **26, 35**: Have `sin(c*log(A*c + 1) + c)` — $\sin(c \cdot \log(cA+1) + c)$. Note that $\log(cA+1)$ is not $\sqrt{A}$, so this cannot equal $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.
- **30**: Has `exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))` — exponential of sin, not sin itself. Cannot match.

**Candidates with log terms** (various): $\log$ terms cannot produce $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.

**Candidates with $A^{c}$ power terms** (3, 8, 11, 12, 13, 17, 18, 21, 24, 29, 32, 33, 36, 37, 39): Power terms like $A^c$ cannot produce $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.

**Candidates with exp terms** (22, 27, 40, 41, 46, 50): Exponential terms like $\exp(A \cdot c)$ or $\exp(c/A^{1/3})$ cannot produce $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.

**Candidates with rational/other terms** (2, 4, 5, 6, 7, 9, 15, 16, 19, 20, 23, 25, 28, 31, 34, 38, 42, 43, 44, 45, 47, 48, 49): None of these contain a $\sin(\sqrt{A})$ term, and none of their building blocks (polynomials, exponentials, logs, rational functions, powers) can combine to produce $\sin(\sqrt{A})$.

The function $\sin(\sqrt{A})$ is a transcendental function that cannot be expressed as any finite combination of the building blocks present in these candidates (polynomials in $A$, $\sqrt{A}$, $\exp(cA)$, $\log(cA+1)$, $\sin(cA+c)$, power functions $A^c$, etc.). The argument $\sqrt{A}$ inside the sine is essential, and no candidate offers $\sin(\sqrt{A})$ or any equivalent form.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT**.

Conclusion: No match

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.33236*A² - 0.33236*A*exp(-0.07071*t) + 0.13650*sin(sqrt(A))`

The GT has three terms:
1. `A²` term (polynomial)
2. `A*exp(c*t)` term (exponential in t, linear in A)
3. `sin(sqrt(A))` term

Let me analyze the key structural elements. The GT contains `sin(sqrt(A))`, which is a very specific basis function. Most candidates don't have `sin(sqrt(A))`.

Let me check which candidates could potentially match by having the right basis functions.

**Common structure in many candidates:** `sqrt(A)*c0*exp(A*c1) + A²*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + ...`

The first term `sqrt(A)*exp(A*c1)`: If we set c1=0, this becomes `c0*sqrt(A)`. But `sqrt(A)` is NOT `sin(sqrt(A))`. These are fundamentally different functions. So `sqrt(A)*exp(A*c1)` with c1=0 gives `sqrt(A)`, which cannot equal `sin(sqrt(A))`.

Can `sqrt(A)*exp(A*c1)` ever equal `sin(sqrt(A))`? No - `exp(A*c1)` is an exponential in A while `sin(sqrt(A))/sqrt(A)` is an oscillating function divided by sqrt(A). These are not equivalent for all A.

So for any candidate to match, it needs a `sin(sqrt(A))` term explicitly, or some combination that can produce it. Since `sin(sqrt(A))` is a transcendental function with specific oscillatory behavior, it cannot be replicated by polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, or rational functions.

Let me check candidates with `sin` terms: Candidates 10, 14, 26, 30, 35.

**Candidate 10:** `...+ c5*sin(A*c6 + c7) + c8` — This is `sin(linear in A)`, not `sin(sqrt(A))`. These are different functions. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 14:** `...+ c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)` — Same issue, `sin(A*c6+c7) ≠ sin(sqrt(A))`. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 26:** `...+ c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8)` — `sin(c6*log(c7*A+1)+c8)`. For this to equal `sin(sqrt(A))`, we'd need `c6*log(c7*A+1)+c8 = sqrt(A)`, which is impossible (log vs sqrt). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 30:** `...+ c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8+c9))` — exponential of sin, not sin(sqrt(A)). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** `...+ c5 + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9)` — Same as 26 with extra constant. **[NO MATCH]**

Since NO candidate contains `sin(sqrt(A))` or any combination that could produce it, and `sin(sqrt(A))` cannot be expressed as any combination of the basis functions present in the candidates (polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, rational functions, `sin(linear)`, `sin(log)`), none of the candidates can match the GT.

Let me verify: the coefficient of `sin(sqrt(A))` in GT is `0.13650 ≠ 0`, so this term cannot be ignored.

Going through all 50 candidates systematically - none contain `sin(sqrt(A))` and none have basis functions that can combine to produce it.
